<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">D+500</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：【档案资料】</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0000"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">罗德岛的老牌干员，年纪在干员中也偏大，因为戴着面具，常给人以难以交流的印象。</font> <font face="宋体">不过交流之后就会发现，本人从不摆出前辈或年长者的架子，是能和年轻人打成一片的活泼大哥哥。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0000"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">黑角的房间里收藏着各式各样的面具，在不同的节日，他会戴上符合节日氛围的面具。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><br/></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">  </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">平时穿戴的似乎是他最喜欢的一款，用他的话说，就是</font><font face="宋体">“俺觉得这一款最搭罗德岛的氛围”。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><br/></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">  </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">顺便一提，面具下并没有见不得人的秘密。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0000"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">黑角的性格中，唯一有些令人在意的地方，就是他似乎有些畏惧夜刀。并不是恐惧，而是不想惹她生气的感觉。这引起了一些比较八卦的干员的注意。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><br/></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">不过无论是两人的履历还是相处模式，都无法看出更多的东西。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">生理系属性：力量</font><font face="宋体">6  敏捷3  耐力6</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">心智系属性：智力</font><font face="宋体">2  感知3  决心2</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'"> </span></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p></td></tr></table>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">生物类型：非人类（泰拉人）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">体型：中型生物（体积</font><font face="宋体">5）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">刻度：源石技力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">攻击：体积，具备</font><font face="宋体">6/6盾牌防御和【格挡】特性的罗德岛干员制式盾牌</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">防御：天生防御</font><font face="宋体">3，2DR/神兵</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">专长：精通盾击</font><font face="宋体">2，以身为盾3，贴身保镖3</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">罗德岛的基石：描述</font><font face="宋体">-即使在开服的少数干员当中，夜刀等2星干员，也被当作路人的象征。如同NPC一样，没有背景，戏份极少，出去个别追求极限操作的高玩或者对于剧情有着别样执着的人之外，根本没有人会注意到他们。但是也就如同凯尔希所言，罗德岛并非是依靠一两个精英干员而建立，而是无数如同夜刀、黑角这样的人建立的。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果</font><font face="宋体">-当黑角帮助友方单位进行协助检定时，可以使友方单位额外获得4DP无名加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">装甲改良：黑角获得</font><font face="宋体">3点天生防御，和基于天生防御的2DR/神兵-已计入防御数值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">悖论模拟</font><font face="宋体">·最速防线：当黑角受到范围能力的影响时，若该能力是造成伤害，则黑角可以以反射动作消耗1点源石技力，使自身触及距离内不超过3名友方单位，获得3点全伤害吸收。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">落叶逐火：该随从可以通过支付差价，升级为</font><font face="宋体">B级随从“火龙S黑角”。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">攻击：体积</font><font face="宋体">2，武器伤害2L，破甲3，基础射程20米的罗德岛干员制式弓箭</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">防御：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">专长：弓箭手</font><font face="宋体">4</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">“据说萨尔贡的弓箭手……”：描述-在《源石尘行动》剧情中，巡林者作为开服就在的2星干员，却意外在这次的联动剧情拿到了相当多的戏份。在这段剧情中，曾经有人向巡林者问起诸多关于萨尔贡的传闻，巡林者都是称其为传说，但后续巡林者与感染生物战斗的内容，也表明这写传闻并非全部都是虚构的。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果</font><font face="宋体">-当巡林者的敏感范围内有友方单位被指定为一次单体远程攻击的目标时，巡林者可以通过一个反射动作/迅捷动作，射出弓箭进行干扰，这会使得攻击者的攻击检定承受巡林者运动技能等级/点无名减值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">老当益壮：巡林者的生命值上限增加</font><font face="宋体">2点；同时自然恢复速度翻倍</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">（短休若原本是</font><font face="宋体">1小时，现在变为30分钟，最低15分钟，长休若原本是8小时，现在变为4小时，最低2小时）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">空射大师：当巡林者攻击处于飞行状态下的单位时，获得【</font><font face="宋体">8点高速优势】。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===========================================================================================================

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">来源：《明日方舟》</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：【客观履历】</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 0pt 0pt 23.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-char-indent-count: 0.0000; mso-para-margin-left: 2.2800gd"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">杜林，罗德岛</font><font face="宋体">A4行动组所属干员。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><br/></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">有着较强的法术天赋，但因自身性格和体质原因无法完全施展。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 0pt 0pt 23.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; mso-char-indent-count: 0.0000; mso-para-margin-left: 2.2800gd"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">极度嗜睡，会随时在任何地方进入睡眠状态，日均睡眠时间远高于干员平均值，但工作却鲜少有缺漏。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：绿色的长发，与之同色的眼瞳</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">精致小巧的五官与一对薄如蝉翼的透明双翅共同构成了别人对眼前这个家伙的第一印象</font><font face="宋体">———妖精</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">无论是显得幼态的外貌，还是整个身体都才堪堪比得上你的拳头般大小，眼前的这个可爱的家伙便是那种仅存在幻想世界中，被称为妖精存在吧？</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">———</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">作为伙伴的话，总是能以魔法来可靠的协助别人，换句话说，正是个擅长使用魔法的家伙</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">除此以外，即使是被弄坏也没关系，就算是被挫骨扬灰也会在重构，但如此惹人怜爱的家伙应该也会被善待，好好</font><font face="宋体">“疼爱”才对吧？</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">性格：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">单从外表上来说，莉耶芙就像是一只普通的妖精那样，可爱的外观下是天真而又善良，珍视自己同伴（？）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">———</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">但这也只是单从外表上来看，而在实际上，伪装对她而言是家常便饭，扭曲的心灵从一开始就让她带上了虚伪的面具</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">喜欢悲剧，喜欢混沌，喜欢看着别人从希望中一下子被打回绝望</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p align="justify" class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">生物类型：黑暗生物、神</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">体型：微型生物（体积</font><font face="宋体">1），但…莉耶芙的体型调整值使用大型生物的</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">攻击：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">防御：防御上获得</font><font face="宋体">9点神圣加值</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">神格存在：莉耶芙似乎是神，但失去了神力，她依然会受到【弑神】的影响。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">臭不要脸：莉耶芙的脸皮很厚</font><font face="宋体">-她的意志池上限提升6点。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); FONT-STYLE: normal; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
